   <script>
    var $DealerInspire_FacebookEvents = {};
 
     jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
 
         $DealerInspire_FacebookEvents = {
 
             facebookPixel: null,
             customEvent: false,
             pixelFired: false,
             events: {
                 EPrice: {
                     name: "EPrice",
                     type: "click",
                     value: ".results_table .primary-cta .button-form, #details-page-ctabox .maincta-row .button-form, .cta-box .vdp-primary.button-form, #cta-mobile-button"
                 },
                 SRP: {
                     name: "SRP",
                     type: "element",
                     value: $(".page-vehicle-results-page")
                 },
                 VDP: {
                     name: "VDP",
                     type: "element",
                     value: $(".page-vehicle-display-page")
                 },
                 Lead: {
                     name: "Lead",
                     type: "url",
                     value: "thank-you"
                 },
                 Parts: {
                     name: "Parts",
                     type: "url",
                     value: "parts"
                 },
                 Service: {
                     name: "Service",
                     type: "url",
                     value:"service"
                 }
             },
 
             init: function() {
                 this.checkCustomEvents();
             },
 
             checkCustomEvents: function() {
                 var self = this;
                 for(eventName in self.events) {
                     if(!self.customEvent) {
                         switch(self.events[eventName].type) {
                             case "element":
                                 if(
                                     typeof self.events[eventName].value !== "undefined"
                                     &&
                                     self.events[eventName].value.length > 0
                                 )
                                     self.customEvent = eventName;
 
                                 break;
                             case "url":
                                 var url = location.href;
                                 var searchString = new RegExp(self.events[eventName].value, "g");
                                 if(url.search(searchString) !== -1)
                                     self.customEvent = eventName;
                                 break;
                             case "click":
                                 var clickEvent = eventName;
                                 $("body").on('click', self.events[eventName].value, function(e) {
                                     var customData = $(e.target).data("vehicle");
                                     console.log(e.target, "The above element was clicked, which sends this FB Remarketing Event: '" + clickEvent + "'");
                                     fbq('trackCustom', clickEvent, customData);
                                 });
                                 break;
                         }
                     }
                 }
 
                 self.fireFacebookEvents();
             },
 
             fireFacebookEvents: function() {
                 var self = this;
 
                 // Enqueue the `fbevents.js` script
                 self.facebookPixels = ["539392409795111"];
                 !function(f,b,e,v,n,t,s)
                 {if(f.fbq)return;n=f.fbq=function(){n.callMethod?
                 n.callMethod.apply(n,arguments):n.queue.push(arguments)};
                 if(!f._fbq)f._fbq=n;n.push=n;n.loaded=!0;n.version='2.0';
                 n.queue=[];t=b.createElement(e);t.async=!0;
                 t.src=v;s=b.getElementsByTagName(e)[0];
                 s.parentNode.insertBefore(t,s)}(window, document,'script',
                 'https://connect.facebook.net/en_US/fbevents.js');
 
                 // Create the `fqb` event
                 for(pixel in self.facebookPixels) {
                     fbq('init', self.facebookPixels[pixel]);
                 }
                 // Handle any found custom events
                 if(self.customEvent) {
                     console.log("FB Remarketing Event: '" + self.customEvent + "'");
                     if(self.customEvent == "VDP" && typeof inventory_localization == "object") {
                         var customData = inventory_localization.vehicle;
                         fbq('trackCustom', self.customEvent, customData);
                         
                     } else {
                         fbq('trackCustom', self.customEvent);
                     }
                     
                     self.pixelFired = true;
                     
                 }
                 // Send the pageview
                 fbq('track', 'PageView');
             }
         };
 
         $DealerInspire_FacebookEvents.init();
     });
   </script>

    <section class="homepage-row" id="welcome-row">
     <div class="top-image">
     </div>
     <div class="container-wide cta-container">
      <div class="row">
       <div class="col-md-8 col-md-offset-2 col-sm-12">
        <div class="content_box text-center">
         <h1>
          Welcome to Mercedes-Benz of San Diego
         </h1>
         <p>
         </p>
         <p>
          For more than 60 years Mercedes-Benz of San Diego has been a premier destination for Southern California buyers in the market for a top-quality luxury vehicle. A proud member of the Penske Auto Group, our dealership is dedicated to providing our neighbors from San Diego, La Jolla, Pacific Beach, Coronado, and Del Mar with a high-quality sales and service experience from start to finish.
         </p>
         <p>
          We offer drivers access to more than
          <a href="/new-vehicles/">
           275 new Mercedes-Benz vehicles
          </a>
          of every description, including the AMG® performance line and a full array of Sprinter and Metris vans ready to be customized with your company’s logo. Drivers can also view some of the latest smart vehicles, as well as more than 100 hand-selected
          <a href="/used-vehicles/">
           pre-owned
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/used-vehicles/certified-pre-owned-vehicles/">
           certified pre-owned options
          </a>
          . Our wide selection ensures that whatever your transportation needs may be, we have you covered.
         </p>
         <p>
          Explore the many
          <a href="/finance/">
           financing
          </a>
          options available with our knowledgeable team of specialists. We can help you review your payment options, compare lease and purchase options, calculate the value of your trade-in vehicle, and even
          <a href="/finance/apply-for-financing/">
           apply for financing online
          </a>
          before you step foot in our showroom.
         </p>
         <p>
          For hands-on service, visit our state-of-the-art Mercedes-Benz authorized
          <a href="/service/">
           service center
          </a>
          . Our factory-trained technicians can perform services ranging from routine maintenance to major collision repair and reunite you with your Mercedes-Benz as quickly as possible.
          <a href="/service/schedule-service/">
           Schedule service
          </a>
          or order parts online today.
         </p>
         <p>
          We invite you to visit our showroom at 4750 Kearny Mesa Rd in San Diego.
          <a href="/contact-us/">
           Contact one of the friendly associates
          </a>
          at Mercedes-Benz of San Diego to learn more about the services we offer and let us show you how car buying was meant to be.
         </p>
         <p>
          <a href="/about-us/">
           Read More
          </a>
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
    </section>

    <script id="penske-pps" type="text/javascript">
     function openChat()
             {
                               // Check for which chat application is on the site
               var $ = jQuery;
               var chats = [
                 "a[onclick*='CNPC.launch(this)']",
                 "a[onclick*='contactatonce']",
                 ".caoChatOnline, .caoChatOnlineMobile",
                 "#wo_online",
                 "#INContent_chatbtn",
                 "#aeChatButtonOnline",
                 ".ae-btn-launcher-content a"
 
               ];
               var chat_found = false;
               $(chats).each(function(i, obj) {
                 if(obj == ".ae-btn-launcher-content a" && !chat_found) {
                   ActivEngage.launchChat(); // use AE method
                   chat_found = true;
                 } else if( $(chats[i]).length > 0) {
                   $(chats[i]).each(function(n, el) {
                     if(!chat_found)
                       $(el).trigger("click"); // Open the found chat by selector
 
                     chat_found = true;
                   });
                 }
               });
                               if(!chat_found) {
                 alert("Sorry, no valid chat applications were found on this page.");
                 $(".pps-buttons")
                   .removeClass("pps-button-4")
                   .addClass("pps-button-3")
                   .find(".button.chat")
                   .hide();
               }
             }
    </script>

 function stopVideoSlide(slide){if(slide.type!="video"){return}

 function pauseVideoSlide(slide){if(slide.type!="video"){return}
 if(slide.player){slide.player.pauseVideo()}}
 function playVideoSlide(slide,swiper){if(slide.type!="video"){return}

 if(event.data===YT.PlayerState.ENDED){if(typeof swiper!='undefined'){swiper.slideNext();swiper.autoplay.start();return}}}}else{if(event.data===YT.PlayerState.ENDED){var seekToTime=(typeof slide.videoStart!='defined'&&slide.videoStart)?slide.videoStart:0;slide.player.seekTo(seekToTime)
 slide.player.playVideo()}}}}})
 function maybeTransitionVideoSlide(){var playerState=slide.player.getPlayerState()
 swiper.autoplay.stop()
 if((slide.videoEnd&&slide.player.getCurrentTime()>=parseInt(slide.videoEnd)-0.5)||playerState==YT.PlayerState.ENDED){if(typeof swiper!='undefined'){swiper.slideNext();swiper.autoplay.start();return true}}}
 function slideAfterDuration(){if(typeof slide.videoEnd!='undefined'){var maybeGoToNextSlideInt=setInterval(function(){while(maybeTransitionVideoSlide(maybeGoToNextSlideInt)){clearInterval(maybeGoToNextSlideInt);break;}},1000);}}}
